  <script>
    $('#mini-spae .x').on('click', function() {
      $('#mini-spae').addClass('closed')
    })
    //respond to events
    window.addEventListener('message', function(event) {
      if (event.data) {
        copy = event.data;
        if (copy.toString().startsWith("Expert")) {
          var title = document.title.split("|").shift().trim().toString(); // get the title of the page
          console.log('Submitted - Request A Call - ' + title);
          dataLayer.push({
            'event': 'Submitted - Request A Call - ' + title
          });
        }

        //new data
        if (copy.toString().startsWith("Request")) {
          console.log('Request A Call');
          dataLayer.push({
            'event': 'Request A Call'
          });
        }
      }
    }, false);
  </script>
